< Review>
First of all, I can't imagine that most of these reviews can be honest ones. Let me start by saying that I really enjoy Burlington for their prices & really good selection. But... The staff is a joke! Mainly the ladies that work @ customer service desk around closing & the evening manager. I shop here often & a cpl days ago, I got home & noticed that they've left the security lock thing on my shoes I just bought. Not really worried about it, I figured I'd return to the store soon as I returned from my business trip in a few days. When I took them back to the store, so they can remove the security tag. I realised I didn't have my receipt on me & probably no longer had it. I didn't think it'd be such a big deal. They made me feel like I was a thief who had stolen these $10 clearance shoes & actually brought them back to the store to kindly ask them to now remove the security tag. I've never been so humiliated in my life & will never shop at Manteca Burlington ever again. This was their mistake, not mine. Yet the manager & girl working service desk last night made me feel as if I did something wrong. Please, please train your checkers to dbl check to make sure they've removed the security tags. I would have much rather gotten a loud siren on way out the day i bought them. That way I wouldn't have had to take them back to remove it & go through this humiliation. Shame on you evening manager!</Review>

< review>
I attened this place last Friday afternoon on my way through town. I do not always go this way but had been working at UC Davis. You can smell the aroma from the smoker at least a block away. This is in a great location easy to find on the corner in a building that appears to be an old gas station who knows i could be wrong. As I walked in I was instantly greated by the staff and talked to in a very personable manner.  The service was very great that alone would make me go back. The lady who was taking orders suggested I try their smoked tri tip sandwich. I was not let down one bit. The tri tip sandwich had the perfect amount of bbq sauce and a great smokey sweet flavorful taste. The sandwich also had grilled onions on it wich was an amazing touch. It is a bit pricey but you get what you pay for. The atmosphere in this place was awesome with locals coming in being greated by name. I loved it i highly recommend trying this place of your ever in town or passing by. Great service great food i will definitely be coming back maybe ill try the pulled pork sandwich next.</review>

<user_name>Gene L< /user_name><Date>1620263821653<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
5/5/21 I'm completely editing my previous review as EVERYONE is entitled to bad days and so many variations of events may have occurred such as new staff or perhaps understaffed that day. We have eaten there so many times since that initial post, Hog Canyon deserves an updated & current review of their establishment. Hog Canyon has the best and juiciest Bacon, Cheeseburgers in Yolo County. Their fries are fantastic! fresh, hot, huge portions that you are left so stuffed with great prices They have great pizza we especially enjoy their combinaions. Our grandkids LOVE the Canadian Pizza. Their crust is very good. Homemade huge salads are very filling. Do NOT Miss their Tri-Tip sandwiches which are packed with excellently cooked Tri-Tip roast cooked over a great oak wood heat source can be smelled a mile away from the beginning of town at the signal light. Which light? THE ONLY LIGHT!!! *lol* Honestly folks I have no horse in this race! They truly have great food and you will NOT be disappointed. After eating here, you'll never want to eat at a fast food joint again!! Their staff are friendly, aim to please and make sure you're their priority and truly believe in customer satisfaction. Oh ya, the milkshakes are bomb, as well as, their homemade cookies. They always sell out of cookies. Thank You Hog Cyn for serving our wonderful little community with excellence.</review>

< Text>
This is a beautiful property and only minutes from Disney! There's a free shuttle that runs every 30 minutes but you can walk it in 10 minutes. The room was nicely furnished and very modern. We did not use the pool, hot tub or fitness center but they were available. The continental breakfast was extensive with eggs, cheese, cereal and all sorts of pastries that were from a local bakery and all was delicious. There are numerous restaurants within walking distance. The staff was very nice and accommodating. They stored our luggage since we arrived early and although there is no office center, the front desk printed our boarding passes for us. I would highly recommend this resort!< /Text>

< review>
I made the reservation for this stay months before my trip, having quite a lengthy discussion with the individual booking the stay. BEWARE of the information you receive! I was told the hotel had a view of California Adventure Cars Land and you could see the nightly fireworks show from the balcony of your room. First of all, there are NO balconies with these rooms. In fact, there are no windows even facing California Adventure. The only available view from ANY room is of the hotel parking lot. What they call 'your room balcony' is the outside walk-way that runs the length and width of the hotel in front of ALL the rooms, just like a Motel 6. If you want to see the fireworks you need to walk to the corner of the outside walkway and peer between the rooms to see the fireworks in the sky, or stand out in the parking lot. Yes, they back up to Cars Land, but what you see from the parking lot is the wood framing holding up the mountain backdrop paintings on the other side. I immediately spoke with the hotel manager when I checked in, expressed my dissatisfaction, and told him I wanted to be compensated in some way for being lied to about both the view to Cars Land and my non-existent balcony. He told me he would look at my charges and that was the end of it. At checkout no compensation was reflected. I'm sure he never gave it a second thought the minute I walked away. Just another lie. Months ago I could have reserved a room with a view at a different hotel, but on check-in it's a little too late for that.
Regardless of everything above, I'm leaving a 3 because there were some very nice things about this hotel. If you stay in one of their premium rooms they deliver their limited continental breakfast to your room each morning. Every night someone comes around to ask if you have any trash you'd like picked up and then gives you a chocolate. The grounds are beautiful and very well maintained. There's a free hotel shuttle that runs every 30 minutes. The rooms are very clean and the staff is extremely friendly. The premium rooms are at the far end of the location which makes them very quiet considering this hotel is right on South Harbor Blvd.</review>

<userid>100628950651846282068<//userid><username>Danny B</username><Time>1541436063929<//Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
I've been staying at the Candy Cane Inn for 25+ years and they NEVER let us down.  The rooms are incredibly clean and believe me, I look in every corner.  Beds are soooo cozy , no comforters and the double-sheet blanket is perfect.  The AC isn't noisy and sleep is good here. :-)

By the way, why wouldn't you pay $20-30 more for a Premium room?  The room is larger, fridge, microwave, free DVD rentals, FREE BREAKFAST delivered to your room in the morning at a time you choose... a nice popcorn bucket full of goodies when you get there, and a 2pm checkout time?  It's a no-brainer!!

NO resort fee.  FREE parking.  FREE Shuttle.  FREE WiFi .  FREE Candy Canes... I mean this is THE resort to stay at!

My tips:   If your feet are tired, take the shuttle.   It's every 30min, but note that between waiting for people to board, it driving slowly around the resort lot to pull out finally, then a u-turn to the resort... etc... within that 15min, you'd already be at the gate of Disneyland.  It's only a 5min walk.

Don't hesitate.  This place is beautifully maintained and a great place to stay.   Keep in mind it's a Motel.  Doors face the outside and yes, because other humans stay there, you'll hear a bit of noise here and there.  For us, no biggie.  It's perfect.  :-)

UPDATE:   A note on the TV... it's nice!  But REALLY limited in it's channels.  No ESPN?  and well, about 8 channels, like the old days!.  No big deal for me, I bring my Roku stick with me and we connected it, connected to their free wifi, and I was good to go.   I'm not sure this is a deal-breaker, but may be for some.<//Review>

< Review>
Rooms are dated, but pleasant enough. The real draw here is the location, which is perfect. There's a free shuttle to Disneyland every half hour, but if you don't want to wait it's just as easy to walk there. There's a 7-11 right next door for all the travel essentials you'll inevitably forget (or if you just want a super cheap hot dog) and there's a few restaurants (including a 24-hour Subway) across the street if you'd rather not eat in the parks. The rates are reasonable, making this a great choice if you are trying to do Disney on a budget.< /Review>

We love to stay at Candy Cane Inn whenever we come to Anaheim and are planning  on going to Disneyland. When they have rooms available this is our first choice. Our last stay was on  4/20/2017 for 3 nights. We stayed in the deluxe room 141. The perks of staying here are many but I'll  mention the few that stand out. Let me start by saying the hospitality of everyone working at Candy Cane Inn is exceptional. For example after our most recent stay we contacted housekeeping regarding us forgetting our pillow there. They quickly retrieved it and mailed it back to us. Very grateful for their kindness and going above the standard to help us with that issue. Moving on not to another benefit of the Candy Cane Inn is its fantastically close location to Disneyland. One can easily walk there or take the complementary shuttle Candy Cane Inn has for their guests and ride to the park if they choose. If you stay in one of the Deluxe rooms breakfast will be brought to your door in the morning if you like. The beds are comfortable. The rooms are quaint and have a simple but homey feel. < Text>
We always stay here during our visit to Disneyland. The main reason is because one of the top wings provides the opportunity to view the fireworks, so we request a room in that wing always. The prices are reasonable for the quality of service provided.  A shuttle departs every half hour to Disneyland.  Each room has an electronic safe.  Pools are clean and the location provides free breakfast to get you going in the morning.  Breakfast includes orange juice, coffee, different cereals, boiled eggs, yogurts, cheese cubes, muffins, bagels, cream cheese, toast with jam, honey or butter, fruits....yum yum. :)  There is also a small shop to purchase a few snacks and souvenirs. Most importantly, you can purchase bottled water too and there is also cucumber flavored ice cold water in the lobby, along with coffee.  Last but not the least, Candy Cane is a walking distance from other places to eat right across the street, and Anaheim Garden Walk is very close. I also saw Cheese Cake Factory and PF Changs just 5 minutes away by walk.  In summary, a very convenient location and parking is free of charge for guests. Laundry is available too.  Candy Cane is a very sweet place to stay and we look forward to visiting Candy Cane again.</Text>

You won't find it with other rewards programs like the major chain hotels, but it quietly beats the competition in location (tucked within 10-minutes walking distance directly behind cars land), in-room amenities (comb, shower cap, mini fridge, and the usual hygiene items like soap, shampoo, conditioner, lotion), table and sitting room chairs, flat screen television, and well-lit. <username>Tom Hay Bauer< /username>< Date>
1523219503727</Date>
<Rate>3</Rate>< review>
I really wanted to like this place, but I came away disappointed. The room had pretty much all the amenities one would like, but it was small and cramped. It was also very dark--partly because of the overhang from the floor above, but also because our handicap room was sandwiched in behind the laundry room and there was absolutely no sunlight at all.  The breakfast was average at best

As for General handicap access, that also leaves much to be desired. There was only one curb cut on our side of the complex and it was quite a ways down from our room. There is also no way to access the main sidewalk in front without walking in the driveway. There are some strictly ornamental sidewalks with curb cuts that go nowhere. It seems like they did not really consider handicap and wheelchair access when they designed this place.< /review>

This was the second time we've stayed at the Candy Cane Inn and I absolutely love it.  The rooms are so nice with the wooden shutters.  There is a coffee maker and refrigerator.  The layout is really nice with the pool and breakfast area in the center.  The shuttle is a real bonus when you are coming back from the parks and exhausted.  The staff is always friendly. Just a note that there isn't an elevator, so you have to lug your bags up the stairs.< /Review>

<Name>Scott Eaton< /Name><Time>1423455615680</Time>< rating>
3</rating>
< review>
Our stay here was really a mixed bag. This is one of the older motor lodges erected around Disneyland. But the owners have done a good job maintaining and updating it over the years. Yet, it still has very tight and limited parking and the basic old characteristic of exterior hallways arranged in a horseshoe around a central pool and office area. The proximity to The Disneyland Resort was great, it was nice to have shuttle service (although we usually just walked), and the morning breakfast was a nice amenity to help get things going in the morning. We would consider going back, but there are definite trade-offs to consider.<//review>

< review>
The perfect spot for a Disney stay. Great location, beautiful (and fragrant) grounds. Good pool and spa area. Rooms are certainly not opulent, but for a family of four worn out from a day at the park, they're just what you need. Wish the beds were a bit bigger (and a bit newer), but for the price, I'm not complaining. The best thing for us, was the breakfast that was brought to our room. It's included in the cost of some rooms and it is highly worth it. Kinda like those fancy places where you order the night before, but minus the $50 or more.< /review>

< review>
The location is right around the corner from the entrance of the parks, it is walking distance (about 15min brisk walk) The breakfast consists of bagels, croissant, choice of 3 cereals fruit & coffee. They also serve hard boiled eggs & cubed cheese. The staff is very helpful & polite. The property has a garden style deco. The rooms are not noise proof. You could hear the children upstairs. The hotel was recommended by AAA, but it was our 2nd choice because of distance (closer). The hotel offers a free shuttle, but I'm not sure if that was part of our pkge. The rooms are smaller than we are used to at previous hotels. Our pkge also had free parking.</review>

<Review>We had positive experiences in the past, but that changed dramatically in 2015, coinciding with new management. They botched our most recent stay in nearly every way possible.

1) Bed bugs! We photographed them, showed them to the front desk, and two staff members accompanied my family and I to the room, verified they were there and only offered to allow us to change rooms (at a downgrade without any refund). Along with two young kids, we hauled all our unpacked things to the other side of the hotel without assistance.

2) No accommodating. We specifically called twice in advance of our stay to ensure we had a bottom floor room for an ADA accommodation since there are no elevators. Both times we were assured it was noted and we'd be taken care of. When we arrived, sure enough they'd booked a top floor room. It took the front desk manager nearly 40 minutes to find an alternative room (at which point the drama referenced above with bed bugs ensued and we had to change rooms yet again).

3) Careless hotel management. I tried reporting this to hotel management. It was delegated lower in every instance. I was encouraged at first by a voice message from a manager, but he said he'd follow up immediately. I called back a day later, he said he didn't have time to get to it and hung up. A week and a half went by, I followed up again. The manager falsely claimed he had called twice. He reported that he'd "done some training" and that they never found bugs. That's not what his staff said in a panic when they were rolling up the sheets and moving us, and that's not what my photos say.

I just wish they'd take action for the good of their customers. There are plenty of other choices just as close, and even closer, to Disneyland. I'd never return and wouldn't be shocked if it gets shuttered so health authorities can compel the insect issue to get taken care of.< /Review>< Pics>

< Review>
My family and I have come to the candy cane inn for a couple generations now. It started with my grandfather when they opened shortly after Disneyland opened back in '55.. then he took my parents, they took me and my brother, I took my wife and now today I'm bringing my little son with me and my wife. Clearly they are doing something right with all the competition around to keep us coming back every time we come here. Sometimes the price is a little high but we try to always come anyway instead of going to other hotels. Ok so for new customers, this hotel is only a couple blocks from both parks, it's one of the most beautiful walks covered in shade and littered with "birds of paradise flowers." The staff are extremely attentive and friendly and the amenities are standard but they feel like they are on another level of quality compared to other hotels. Their breakfast in the morning, every morning ranges and sometimes it is better than other days. But I can guarantee that you will have a decent selection no matter what day, of multiple items..it just may not be a hot breakfast type of menu. We still thoroughly enjoy it with the breakfaat the way it is and with the comfortable beds and upgraded rooms...the rooms have been upgraded tremendously since our last trip to Disneyland and we love the changes. They feel refreshed and cleaner as well as more modern. I give this hotel a rating of 5 stars... Not because of luxury but more for convenience and price considering the convenient location being so close to Disneyland. We walk because it's so close to the park but I should mention that they STILL have a shuttle going back and forth every 30 minutes even with their hotel being this close to the park... This tells you everything about how they feel about their guests right there... If they still pay to shuttle guests every 30 minutes all day every day an pay an employee for said services just to make guests happy... This hotel is amazing. That's all I have to say about that.< /Review>

<Review>Okay, this review is long overdue.

Came to Anaheim during Labor Day weekend with my relatives.  We stayed here for the duration to be close to Disneyland.  Only a 10-minute walk to the park entrance.  Not to mention that they have a private bus that leaves every 30 minutes if you don't want to put in any extra legwork.

As for the actual place, the rooms were great.  Comfy beds, hardwood laminated floors, and shuttered windows.  So pretty much NO real risks of bed bugs.

Then there's the staff and their accomadations.  My sister had a stroller on reserve for use during the duration of our visit.  They were nice enough to let us leave it in front office when we didn't need it.  The staff were VERY accomadating, especially in helping to get our flight itinerary printed for our flight home.

Lest I forget, they serve a lovely, fully complementary, Continental Breakfast.  No room service, but we weren't really expecting any to begin with.  Still, the breakfast was great.  Sprawls of fresh fruit, hard-boiled eggs, bagels (and bagel oven), muffins, donuts, cheese cubes.  That's not even getting into the coffee and OJ machines they have.  Or the cereal dispenser outside, with chilled milk in glass pitchers, served on ice.

Bottom line, if you don't mind covering your own lunch and dinner,  I can't recommend Candy Cane Inn highly enough.  I promise, you won't be disappointed.< /Review>< Pics>

Overall a very positive experience!

Location: Just a few minutes walk from Disneyland.
A major plus is their dedicated shuttle to and from Disneyland Park for those times where you just can't walk anymore!

Free Breakfast! Our premium room came with it delivered right to our door, but everyone has access to complimentary breakfast options starting at 6:30am in the front building.

Pool is open until 11pm, there are two jacuzzis as well.

Wonderful and fast service when we requested a pull-away bed or asked for more pillows.

They even have free Candy Canes and pens shapes like them too!<//review>

<user_id>105160710068638891907<//user_id><user_name>Benjamin Kitt<//user_name>< date>
1501634061090<//date>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
What a great little hotel! You're probably thinking of staying here to visit Disneyland. If you've stayed on Disney properties, the Candy Cane is equivalent to a moderate resort. The rooms are clean and of a reasonable size with great toiletries and good TV offerings. The beds are comfortable with crisp white sheets. Each room has an in wall heater/air conditioner. The free breakfast consists of a selection of pastries, bagels and donuts along with cold cereals, yogurts, cheese, hard boiled eggs and various other bits and pieces. Juices, milk and hot drinks are provided, including hot chocolate. The fresh, chewy bagels and sweet, fluffy donuts are excellent. The pool is small and plain but deep and clean with a hot tub area and a toddler area. Don't expect to do laps in it, but it's a great place to cool off with the family. The walk to Disneyland from the hotel is about 10 minutes at a moderate pace. The hotel does provide a shuttle but it takes longer than walking - I'd skip it. If you can, get a room that's close to the entrance. Not only do you have great access to the pool and breakfast but you'll be glad to save those extra few hundred steps after a long day in the parks. Overall a great stay, recommended!<//Review>

<Text>Candy Cane is one of my favorite places to stay when visiting Disneyland. The hotel grounds are beautiful, the staff is friendly and helpful, the rooms are very nice and the location is great. Walking to Disneyland is very doable, the walk is easy and quite safe. But if you don't want to walk there is a free shuttle service that is great and always on time. Rooms are nice, clean and we'll appointed. The beds are very comfortable and the pillows are amazing. I sleep better here than I do at home. Shower water pressure is great. < Rate>
4< /Rate>
< review>
Reminds me of a hotel in the London area. Family owned, they have taken great care to make sure the property and rooms are clean and welcoming. Most areas in the US would just demolish places like this instead of maintaining the original integrity. We stayed 2 nights in a chain hotel and then 1 night here, because of availability. More value here, plus you are supporting local businesses. Employees were noticeably more pleasent and happy than the chain, could be the personal investment. The hotel is very close to Disney entrances but offers a clean shuttle back and forth. There is a Walgreens and CVS even closer which in convenient. Rooms are not my style with the pastel pallets and lower ceilings but they are clean. The air circulation in the room is not ideal, especially with my two teens in the room. Febreeze could have helped, keep that in mind if there are more than 2 of you in a room. This was our first visit to this hotel and I was very pleased. I will recommend it to friends and return if I have the opportunity.<//review>

< Review>
Came here for the same reason in 2012 for the same reason everyone does. Proximity to Disneyland. It does not get much closer, and the hotel provides a shuttle to the east entrance. Stayed 3 nights at this place. It is pricey considering the size of the rooms, but the rooms are clean and fairly nice. The hotel outside is gorgeous and the pool is great. Had a little trouble connecting to the wi-fi from the room on my tablet, but the room we were in as toward the back. I would walk up to the pool area and it would work fine. Breakfast there is mediocre but the hotel is next door to the 7-Eleven and reasonable walking distance to several restaurants. Service was great. If you are not on a total budget, Candy Cane is the place to go.</Review>

<user_name>Brookes Stepp< /user_name>< review>
Honestly we had passed up on this hotel for many years simply because it wasn't a large chain,  boy was that a mistake.  We decided to extend our trip an extra night and gave this place a shot.  Not only were the staff extremely helpful but they were very courteous and it made the difference.  Let me be clear,  our room was a very standard no frills room as you would expect for the price but it was properly maintained and very very clean.  Their breakfast was very good compared to others I've seen.  Free shuttle that runs every 30 minutes unlike some places that have a handful of drop offs and pickups or those that make you ride the ART.  Free parking!!! I don't understand where hotels get off charging upwards of $20 for parking when you've dropped a few hundred  bucks for a room there.  The only negative I have to mention was the free WiFi internet,  it took me an hour to get it to work and once I did I was greeted by some serious warnings indicating their security had been compromised or something.  I simply didn't use it after that.  Oh and unlike some of the other hotels across the street from Disneyland,  it appears that these people care about building up repeat customers since they are happy to offer discounts on your next visit.  I have been staying at Park Vue for years and they've never offered me anything in the form of a discount or upgrade.</review>

<Review>I have only the best to say about this hotel! Highly recommended! So happy we chose the Candy Cane Inn for our trip to Disneyland. Every employee we came across was very friendly and willing to go out of their way to do whatever they could for us. Some highlights: The welcoming exterier of the rooms, beautiful vegatation and the scent of flowers everywhere, the most absolutly comfortable rooms (loved the beds!), the awesome free morning breakfast, with so many choices, and the free shuttle straight to Disneyland and back. No sitting through 8 different hotel stops before you get to your own!
